<Review>I recently bought work van to start a business for myself. The van did not pass smog and needed some smog repairs. After failing the smog test, I immediately drove it to Midas, because I am still rather new to the West Side, and I haven't used any other mechanics in this area. I assumed that Midas was qualified to do the repairs...

I explained my situation to David at the front desk, and he reassured me multiple times that everything would be taken care of. I was very clear that I needed the vehicle to pass smog, and that smog repairs were my only reason for coming to the shop.

The following day I received a call from David informing me that the van had a couple check engine lights, one for a MAF sensor and another for misfires. He explained that the vehicle had not received new spark plugs in a long time and was probably misfiring due to needing a tune up. He convinced me to spend a few hundred bucks on a tune up and said I would be good to go. They also replaced a MAF and something else... After it was all said and done the repairs were just under $700.

I take the vehicle to get the smog test done and it fails again. I immediately call Midas and they assure me that I have not driven the van enough to reset the monitors, and to drive the van 60 miles, then I will be good to go. So I do this, then take it back to Midas and have them check it again, and it is still showing check engine lights. They tell me that I still have not driven the van enough, after I drove it close it 100 miles. So I drove it another 75-100 miles and brought it back again. The check it again and the check engine light still wont go away.

David recommends me to LARSENS AUTOMOTIVE (best thing that came out of this whole experience, highly recommend LARSEN AUTOMOTIVE)

I go to Larsen's and wow, what a breath of fresh air. I cannot even begin to explain the difference in quality of mechanics, service, and expertise. The guys at Larsen's really know what they are talking about. The first thing that they told me at Larsen's is that only CALIFORNIA CERTIFIED SMOG REPAIR STATIONS should be doing the work. Because if it does not pass, which it did not, the repairs must have been done at a certified shop in order to have the Smog waivered.....

WOW. Thanks a lot Midas. Now the $700 I spent is worthless to the DMV because you are NOT CERTIFIED to do smog repairs. I must spend another $650 at a CERTIFIED smog repair station...Larsen's informs me that because I already spent the money, my best option would be to see if Midas can complete the repairs and get the vehicle to pass smog.

Larsen's preforms their own diagnostic test and explains that the problems causing the vehicle to fail the smog test were NEVER properly diagnosed or addressed, and that all they did was do a tune up and call it a day. Larsen's had a very clear understanding of the problems and what steps needed to be taken to resolve them.

I went back to Midas with this information and they agreed to look at the vehicle further. After several days they called me to explain that they had given up. They were unable to solve the issues and were not going to continue working on the vehicle.

They then returned the van to me with less than 1 quart of oil in the engine. When I asked about this the mechanic explain that he checked the oil, so it must have all leaked out. So I asked him if he had a puddle of oil anywhere with 4 quarts of oil on the ground, but he said no. So I am not sure where he thinks 4 quarts of oil disappeared to between the time he claims to have checked it and the time they gave it back to me. (Grade A mechanic)

So here I am now stuck with a van that will not pass smog. It still needs over $1k in repairs, and the DMV will not waiver the test because the repairs were not preformed at a certified repair station.

Thanks a lot Midas. I will be pursuing this is court for misrepresentation.</Review>< Gmap_id>

<name>Jonathan Ford< /name><date>1589329441385<//date><rate>1<//rate>< review>
I almost never write a negative review, but this place has given me one of the worst customer service experiences I've ever had.

We "inherited" an elderly dog, Bella, from friends of ours who could no longer keep her.  We mostly took her to make sure she was looked after and had a good home.  She came with some medical conditions we didn't expect.  One of which is she accidentally pees while she sleeps and has difficulty with urination while awake.  Our previous vet was able to help our dog with some prescription medicine we give her twice a day.  About once a year she needed a $50 check up to make sure there weren't any complications.

After we moved we needed a new vet.  Summer Hills was right down the street and had okay reviews.  My first experience with Summer Hills was them pressuring my wife into over $500 in other expenses when she took her in for a $50 check up with heavy handed scare tactics.  Expensive (not the normal) blood test, heart worm medication, urinalysis, etc.  They implied that if she didn't purchase these the dog could die, and pushed the guilt pretty hard.

I called and told them that was not what we wanted and they needed to cancel all the test the reception was very passive aggressive and rude and had an attitude of "well i guess if you don't care about your dog I can cancel the test"

Last week we noticed that Bella's medication hadn't arrived in the mail like it typically does.  Summer Hills denied the prescription refill without notifying us it was time for our Bella to get her check up.  Mildly irritating but fine so far, we scheduled an appointment for a week later.

When I arrive a week later the reception told me that they have no appointment scheduled for Bella and we would have to bring her back another time.  I tried to talk to her, to see if we could somehow get her in today, that I would be willing to wait.  She was incredibly rude, passive aggressive, and belittling.  After being polite but assistant she checked with the vet if Bella could be seen today because we were nearly out of her medication and didn't want her going longer without it.  The vet sent her back to ask if we had collected Bella's urine sample.  When we first scheduled her appointment there was no mention of collecting a urine sample.

I told her I don't want to run any additional test, I just want her to get her medication so she can be taken care of.  She claimed it was the law that they give her a urinalysis, to which I replied "You guys consistently try to pressure me into additional test and preventative treatments, I just want my dog to get a check up so I can get her medication.  You renewed her prescription last time without urinalysis, and her previous vet renewed it for years without urinalysis.  Does a law really requires urinalysis for this?"  At this point she got angry and told me that the vet wouldn't be seeing Bella without a urine sample.

I said fine, how do I collect this sample.  At this point I just wanted to get my dog her medication.  She responded in voice like she was talking to a small child, "I'll be happy to tell you how to collect urine, as soon as you change your tone of voice".  I at no point yelled, raised my voice, or was anything but polite and courteous to this lady whom had been very rude to me.  I told her that this is a frustrating situation, my appointment got canceled somehow, and asked her if she could please just tell me how to collect my dogs urine so I can get her her medication ASAP.  She said "I'd be happy to as soon you're ready to let me do my job."  Again I didn't interrupt her, speak rudely to her, raise my voice, or do anything that could be construed as aggressive in any way.

At that point I told her no thank you, I'll be looking for another vet.  Honestly I'm still kind of blown away by this whole thing.  This is some of the worst customer service i've ever had.  And now I need to try and find another vet to get my dog her medication.<//review>

<text>We had our company holiday luncheon here. They have valet parking as it is difficult to find a place to park due to the close proximity to other businesses nearby.  Plan accordingly so you can find a parking spot.
We had an 11:45 a.m. reservation and the restaurant was already packed and hopping with other couples and small groups having lunch.  There is not much room inside for a large party (we had nine in our party) to wait to be seated.
It appeared chaotic with wait staff walking back and forth along with the busboys bring bread and water to the tables. It was quite noisy, and cramped (tables close together) that we had a hard time hearing each other talk.
We were seated and given menus, water was poured and bread delivered. No one told us the daily specials or what the soup of the day was. Our waiter never told us his name.
We started off with two orders of friend calamari. Cooked to perfection. Tender morsels of goodness.  Served with aioli sauce and what appeared to be sweetened ketchup. It would have been better had there been horseradish in it to give it zip.
We ordered the Kobe Steak. Who serves Kobe steak with sauce poured over it? It came with a handful of raw baby spinach and mashed potatoes.
The Cannelloni was just that. Two freshly made crepe-like pastas and sauce. No side salad, no vegetable saute. Just the pasta. Very unfinished. It would have benefited from some freshly grated parmesan.
The French Dip was okay. Sparse on the meat. Served with French fries and au jus.
The Grilled Prawn Salad would have been great had the prawns been freshly grilled. Everything on the salad was delicious. We think that the prawns were what gave us issues later that afternoon.
We had the Pasta special which had one asparagus spear sliced in a delicious tomato sauce and freshly cooked prawns.
We ordered some desserts and had a rude woman, not our waiter, serve them to us. She was like a slap-in-the-face when she spoke to our group. To top it off she also delivered dirty spoons to us.
Banana Fosters Bread Pudding. It was popping hot served with a melting scoop of vanilla ice cream. Definitely enough for two to share.
The Chocolate Lava Cake was dry and the ice cream had slipped off and was melting on the plate. Not a favorite.
It's the holiday season and we will not be returning to Zinfandel Grille for future company gatherings. They will not miss our business as the restaurant was packed on a Tuesday for lunch.< /text><UserId.>101761588418388535261< /UserId.>< gmapID>

The Zinfandel Grille has always been on the family restaurants list. The pizzas are delicious with the finest ingredients for the break. The pizzas are scrumptious and they are a very good dish. <Name>Sarahjane Dalley</Name>< Review>
The New England style clam chowder is always delicious.  The fresh bread with the balsamic vinegar and olive oil (with herbs and fresh garlic is also always delicious. My wife had the pork chop(wonderfully tender)with polenta cake and green beans. She was duly pleased.  I ordered the filet and substituted mashed potatoes and spinach for the offered fingerling potatoes and asparagus. Sadly my steak was very fatty and overcooked.  I sent it back.  It took the entire meal to get the replacement which I had boxed to go at that point.  This is not the first time they have served an overcooked steak.  The GM brought the box to our table and said "sorry you didn't like the first one" I let him know the chef agreed that it was not cooked properly and was inordinately fatty.  He did not offer to take anything off the bill or even offer a dessert on the house for the error.  The food is generally very good and the service good, although the entrees frequently are slow to arrive. Really not impressed with the customer service after they screwed up our meal however and they did the same thing last time I had to send my food back.  Not my idea of the way a patron should be treated in this situation.</Review>

<GmapID>0x809ada561433f66d:0xdd4b7deee2bc684e< /GmapID>< Rating>
4</Rating>
< user_name>
myna nacare<//user_name>
<Pics>None< /Pics>< review>
Great local place to eat for a treat!

Popular so make a reservation or prepare to either eat outside or wait. For the same reason be patient when parking. There are many tasty selections and specials, live music, and newcomer discounts (hint: email list) so it's a low-risk venture to try.

The Friday night we dined we were spared a 20 minute wait and seated immediately outside since we had no reservations, passing by fresh food preparation on the way. Staff was friendly, attentive without being overbearing, and quite accommodating. Lots of good teamwork noted with service.

The atmosphere is fresh and light despite activity, unpretentious but stylish, and in true California mode is appropriate for the casual dresser to the gussied up romantic date. Not really a kid place, unless you're with a big party but they also do banquets.

The manager let us know there are 22 different kinds of (mostly non-vocalist) musical groups there on Friday and Saturdays. The volume was just right as backdrop music. On Wednesdays they have a myriad of specials and shenanigans offered.

Our dishes were superbly done, with clear but subtle flavors and gently sauced. They make nearly everything from scratch and are more than happy to customize your meal. I had Salmon with Polenta cake and mixed squash. It was delicious! (And I don't usually like squash) My friend had beautifully done Pork Chops served with a creamy butternut squash. Kinda made me wish we could trade. Or eat both :] Plus they made me a killer Old Fashioned with my favorite Woodford Bourbon, thanks to our fabulous server, Amy!!

If the prices were a little lower here it'd become dangerous for me! LOL
Even after just one visit, I declare this one a total win!< /review>
